# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="f1215-105">Veraltete Member in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f1215-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f1215-106">In diesem Artikel werden die Typmember aufgeführt, die in .NET Framework 4.5 und höheren Versionen veraltet sind.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f1215-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f1215-107">Typmember werden nach Assembly gruppiert.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f1215-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f1215-108">In diesem Artikel werden die Member veralteter Typen nicht aufgeführt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f1215-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f1215-109">Eine Liste veralteter Typen finden Sie unter [Veraltete Typen](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f1215-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
